[giow] (2) Make sure plugins for <object> aren't instantiated before the <param>s are read. This makes <object> slower (which we avoided with <video>, for instance), but it appears to be needed for back-compat.
Fixing http://www.w3.org/Bugs/Public/show_bug.cgi?id=9014
